42 #include <cassert>
43 
44 // Need to see definition of JLexer class before defining the
45 // next actions.
46 // This will mean this file is included twice in JLexer.cpp. This
47 // should do no harm...
48 #include "JLexer.h"
49 
50 // The lexical analyser passes some information through to
51 // the parse store to be integrated with parse information before
52 
53 inline void IncrementCount(LexicalCount tc)
54 {
55  assert(ParseStore::currentInstance()!=NULL);
56  ParseStore::currentInstance()->IncrementCount(tc);
57 }
58 
59 inline void endOfLine(JLexer &lexer)
60 {
61  assert(ParseStore::currentInstance()!=NULL);
62  ParseStore::currentInstance()->endOfLine(lexer.line());
63  lexer.newline();
64  lexer.skip();
65 }
66 
67 inline void endOfCommentLine(JLexer &lexer)
68 {
69  IncrementCount(tcCOMLINES);
70  endOfLine(lexer);
71 }
